              <h1 class="post-title entry-title">
               7 New Premium WordPress Themes for Restaurants &amp; Cafes
              </h1>
              <div class="post-body entry-content" id="post-body-8378198024480508112">
               <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                <div style="text-align: justify;">
                 <span href="http://wordpresspremiumthemes.quora.com/#" id="__w2_alUgVE3_toggle_link">
                  <span id="ld_qgimwy_1253">
                   <span id="ld_qgimwy_1254">
                    <span class="inline_editor_value">
                     This is a collection of
                     <b>
                      WordPress themes for restaurants, cafes, pubs, coffee shops
                     </b>
                     , and other
                     <b>
                      food and beverage websites
                     </b>
                     .
 If you run a restaurant these days its critical to have an online 
presence. WordPress makes it easy and inexpensive to create a 
professional and attractive website.
                     <br/>
                     <br/>
                     The
                     <b>
                      WordPress themes
                     </b>
                     below are specifically designed for restaurant and cafes websites and include a range of restaurant specific features such as
                     <b>
                      custom menu templates, integrated
                     </b>
                     <b>
                      Google
                     </b>
                     <b>
                      maps, contact information section, daily specials, photo galleries,
                     </b>
                     <b>
                      Facebook
                     </b>
                     <b>
                      fan page compatibility
                     </b>
                     and some even include a
                     <b>
                      built in reservation system
                     </b>
                     .
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </span>
                </div>
                <h2>
                 1. Fine Food - Restaurant Responsive WordPress Theme
                 <span class="qlink_container">
                  <a class="external_link" data-tooltip="attached" href="http://themeforest.net/item/fine-food-restaurant-responsive-wordpress-theme/4443941?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Info
                  </a>
                 </span>
                 |
                 <span class="qlink_container">
                  <a class="external_link" data-tooltip="attached" href="http://themeforest.net/item/fine-food-restaurant-responsive-wordpress-theme/full_screen_preview/4443941?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   Demo
                  </a>
                 </span>
                </h2>
                <br/>
                <div dir="ltr" style="text-align: left;" trbidi="on">
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8zkQ2k4ev-M/UhiComT8vBI/AAAAAAAABLc/eNX5X04zJrU/s1600/Restaurant+Responsive+WordPress+Theme+download+free.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-8zkQ2k4ev-M/UhiComT8vBI/AAAAAAAABLc/eNX5X04zJrU/s1600/Restaurant+Responsive+WordPress+Theme+download+free.jpg"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <span href="http://wordpresspremiumthemes.quora.com/#" id="__w2_alUgVE3_toggle_link">
                   <span id="ld_qgimwy_1253">
                    <span id="ld_qgimwy_1254">
                     <span class="inline_editor_value">
                      <b>
                       Fine Food
                      </b>
                      is a Responsive WordPress theme suitable for any kind of restaurant, 
hotel, caf, coffee shop, spa and similar websites that needs a feature
 rich and beautiful presence online. The main features, which are 
extremely important and super useful are, 3 features including Events 
Calendar &amp; Management, Menu &amp; Recipe and Facebook fan page 
compatibility.
                     </span>
                    </span>
                   </span>
                  </span>
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                  2. The Restaurant: Classic Edition
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" data-tooltip="attached" href="http://themeforest.net/item/the-restaurant-classic-edition/4047474?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" data-tooltip="attached" href="http://www.redfactory.nl/themes/switcher/?theme=therestaurantclassic&amp;ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-02ece102602082ea8b34ab8f9d8e74c7"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   The Restaurant: Classic Edition
                  </b>
                  is created for anyone looking to start their own restaurant website. 
This premium theme includes a couple of advanced features such as a
                  <b>
                   beautyful sliding menucard
                  </b>
                  with an easy-to-use
                  <b>
                   menucard builder
                  </b>
                  . You can make as many different menucards as you want!
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  This
 premium theme is a fully flexible and responsive WordPress Theme, 
meaning it will work on your tablet and mobile phone and fully 
compatible with
                  <b>
                   translation plugins
                  </b>
                  like
                  <b>
                   WPML
                  </b>
                  .
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                 </h2>
                 <h2>
                  3. Coffee Shop - Responsive WP Theme For Restaurant
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/coffee-shop-responsive-wp-theme-for-restaurant/4038168?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/coffee-shop-responsive-wp-theme-for-restaurant/full_screen_preview/4038168?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-d57186efdeec0091d22e2577e155e143"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   Coffee Shop
                  </b>
                  is a premium responsive WP template for Cafes and Bistros website. 
After purchasing this theme, you will receive the WordPress version as 
well as 5 PSD files. They are all layered and well organized in folder 
for easier use.
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   Main features
                  </b>
                  : Fully Localized, Menu Custom 
Post Type, Events Custom Post Type, Staff Custom Post Type, Custom 
Widgets For Recent News, Menu &amp; Events, Options to change any 
colors and many more.
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                 </h2>
                 <h2>
                  4. Delimondo Responsive Wordpress Theme
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" data-tooltip="attached" href="http://themeforest.net/item/delimondo-responsive-wordpress-theme-5-styles/3992840?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/delimondo-responsive-wordpress-theme-5-styles/full_screen_preview/3992840?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-6df76b133c05eb5d399103669fdc56c9"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <b>
                  Delimondo is a powerful WordPress Template
                 </b>
                 built for restaurants and food lovers. This template is built upon
                 <b>
                  bootstrap framework
                 </b>
                 and is fully responsive. It adapts to window resolution and looks fantastic on all devices including ipad and iphone.
                 <br/>
                 It has 5 awesome pre-styled restaurant versions.
                 <br/>
                 <h2>
                  5. Eatery - Responsive Restaurant WordPress Theme
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/eatery-responsive-restaurant-wordpress-theme/3469316?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://demo.themovation.com/?theme=eatery&amp;ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-0e49c0be19c2f44cea9791d8d4e845b7"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   Eatery is a premium Restaurant WordPress theme
                  </b>
                  created for restaurants and cafs. It features a very clean,
                  <b>
                   responsive design
                  </b>
                  that is perfect for creating a professional image of your restaurant or business. Its easy to customize with
                  <b>
                   awesome features
                  </b>
                  (like 6 beautiful theme skins!) and has plenty of
                  <b>
                   easy to use shortcodes and tools
                  </b>
                  . Eatery is also
                  <b>
                   fully compatible with WPML
                  </b>
                   The WordPress Multilingual Plugin.
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                 </h2>
                 <h2>
                  6. Linguini: Restaurant Responsive WordPress Theme
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/linguini-restaurant-responsive-wordpress-theme/1945015?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/linguini-restaurant-responsive-wordpress-theme/full_screen_preview/1945015?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-6c5dcb75ebf37ca454396a84d0ed7b90"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  Linguini is a theme perfect fit for the restaurants, pubs, bars, wineries and other companies offering foods and drinks.
                  <b>
                   Linguini theme
                  </b>
                  offers an excellent system for administration menu cards (food menu, 
drink menu) and photo galleries. The theme is highly optimized for 
search engines and has excellent SEO options like adding your own 
keywords and meta descriptions for each page, post or menu item. 
Linguini is a fully responsive theme for WordPress, which adapting 
display to all devices (screen, widescreen, iPhone, iPad, Android  
correct displaying in each device, really)  try to resize your browser
 window.
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  If you need a website that will perfectly represent your 
business, Linguini is the right choice for you. Working with Linguini 
is very simple and intuitive, even a beginner can handle it.
                 </div>
                 <h2>
                 </h2>
                 <h2>
                  7. Pluto Fullscreen Cafe and Restaurant
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/pluto-fullscreen-cafe-and-restaurant/534738?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Info
                   </a>
                  </span>
                  |
                  <span class="qlink_container">
                   <a class="external_link" href="http://themeforest.net/item/pluto-fullscreen-cafe-and-restaurant/full_screen_preview/534738?ref=datasata" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                    Demo
                   </a>
                  </span>
                 </h2>
                 <div>
                  <img class="qtext_image zoomable_in zoomable_in_feed" src="http://qph.is.quoracdn.net/main-qimg-cb3bb16a1a3d6e7eef9c7d3fe02e3b8d"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: justify;">
                  <b>
                   Pluto
                  </b>
                  is the
                  <b>
                   Wordpress theme for Cafe and Restaurant
                  </b>
                  built with latest Wordpress features. Custom Post Type, Skins &amp; 
Colors, Extensive admin panel etc. It has Drag &amp; drop Homepage 
Contents Manager, Control and order which content to show on homepage 
from Admin panel and Translation ready plugin.
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
